post /api/v1/accounts/{id}/block
(apiV1AccountsIdBlockPost)
Block the given account. Clients should filter statuses from this account if received (e.g. due to a boost in the Home timeline).

Path parameters

id (required)
Path Parameter — The id of the account in the database default: null

Return type

Relationship

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "note" : "note",
  "notifying" : true,
  "domain_blocking" : true,
  "endorsed" : true,
  "followed_by" : true,
  "muting" : true,
  "requested" : true,
  "blocked_by" : true,
  "blocking" : true,
  "following" : true,
  "muting_notifications" : true,
  "id" : "id",
  "showing_reblogs" : true
}

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "error_description" : "error_description",
  "error" : "error"
}

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

Successfully blocked, or account was already blocked Relationship

401

Invalid or missing Authorization header Error
Up

post /api/v1/accounts/{id}/follow
(apiV1AccountsIdFollowPost)
Follow the given account. Can also be used to update whether to show reblogs or enable notifications.

Path parameters

id (required)
Path Parameter — The id of the account in the database default: null

Consumes

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/form-data

Request body

Body Parameter —

Return type

Relationship

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "note" : "note",
  "notifying" : true,
  "domain_blocking" : true,
  "endorsed" : true,
  "followed_by" : true,
  "muting" : true,
  "requested" : true,
  "blocked_by" : true,
  "blocking" : true,
  "following" : true,
  "muting_notifications" : true,
  "id" : "id",
  "showing_reblogs" : true
}

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "error_description" : "error_description",
  "error" : "error"
}

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

Successfully followed, or account was already followed Relationship

403

Trying to follow someone that you block or that blocks you Error

get /api/v1/accounts/{id}/identity_proofs
(apiV1AccountsIdIdentityProofsGet)
Array of IdentityProof

Path parameters

id (required)
Path Parameter — The id of the account in the database default: null

Return type

array[IdentityProof]

Example data

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

Statuses posted to the given account. Public (for public statuses only), or user token + read:statuses (for private statuses the user is authorized to see)

401

Instance is in whitelist mode or running a version of Mastodon older than 2.7.0, and the Authorization header is invalid or missing Error

404

Account is deleted or does not exist Error

410

Account is suspended

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

Success
Up 
post /api/v1/admin/reports/{id}/assign_to_self
(apiV1AdminReportsIdAssignToSelfPost)
Claim the handling of this report to yourself.

Path parameters

id (required)
Path Parameter — ID of the report default: null

Return type

AdminReport

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

Success AdminReport
Up 
get /api/v1/admin/reports/{id}
(apiV1AdminReportsIdGet)
View information about the report with the given ID.

Path parameters

id (required)
Path Parameter — ID of the report default: null

Return type

AdminReport

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

Success AdminReport
Up 
post /api/v1/admin/reports/{id}/reopen
(apiV1AdminReportsIdReopenPost)
Mark a report as resolved with no further action taken.

Path parameters

id (required)
Path Parameter — ID of the report default: null

Return type

AdminReport

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

Success AdminReport
Up 
post /api/v1/admin/reports/{id}/resolve
(apiV1AdminReportsIdResolvePost)
Mark a report as resolved with no further action taken.

Path parameters

id (required)
Path Parameter — ID of the report default: null

Return type

AdminReport

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

Success AdminReport
Up 
post /api/v1/admin/reports/{id}/unassign
(apiV1AdminReportsIdUnassignPost)
Unassign a report so that someone else can claim it.

Path parameters

id (required)
Path Parameter — ID of the report default: null

Return type

AdminReport

get /api/v1/conversations
(apiV1ConversationsGet)
Show conversation.

Query parameters

limit (optional)
Query Parameter — Max number of results to return. Defaults to 20. default: 20
max_id (optional)
Query Parameter — Return results older than ID default: null
since_id (optional)
Query Parameter — Return results newer than ID default: null
min_id (optional)
Query Parameter — Return results immediately newer than ID default: null

Return type

array[Conversation]

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
[ {
  "unread" : true,
  "last_status" : {
    "pinned" : true,
    "in_reply_to_id" : "in_reply_to_id",

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

Success.

401

Invalid or missing Authorization header Error
Up 
delete /api/v1/conversations/{id}
(apiV1ConversationsIdDelete)
Remove converstation

Path parameters

id (required)
Path Parameter — ID of the conversation in the database default: null

Return type

Object

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "error_description" : "error_description",
  "error" : "error"
}

Example data

Content-Type: application/json

  "error_description" : "error_description",

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.

Success. Object

get /api/v1/directory
(apiV1DirectoryGet)
List accounts visible in the directory.

Query parameters

limit (optional)
Query Parameter — How many accounts to load. Default 40. default: 40
offset (optional)
Query Parameter — How many accounts to skip before returning results. Default 0. default: 0
order (optional)
Query Parameter — the active to sort by most recently posted statuses (default) or new to sort by most recently created profiles. default: active
local (optional)
Query Parameter — Only return local accounts. default: null

array[Account]

(apiV1DomainBlocksPost)

"Block a domain to:

  • hide all public posts from it
  • hide all notifications from it

get /api/v1/notifications
(apiV1NotificationsGet)
Notifications concerning the user. This API returns Link headers containing links to the next/previous page. However, the links can also be constructed dynamically using query params and id values.

Query parameters

limit (optional)
Query Parameter — Max number of results to return. Defaults to 20. default: 20
max_id (optional)
Query Parameter — Return results older than ID default: null
since_id (optional)
Query Parameter — Return results newer than ID default: null
min_id (optional)
Query Parameter — Return results immediately newer than ID default: null
exclude_types (optional)
Query Parameter — Array of types to exclude (follow, favourite, reblog, mention, poll, follow_request) default: null
account_id (optional)
Query Parameter — Return only notifications received from this account default: null

Return type

array[Notification]

Query Parameter — Return results newer than ID default: null
min_id (optional)

401

Invalid or missing Authorization header Error

404

422

Status is not owned by you, or is not public. You cannot pin one of your private statuses because private statuses cannot be fetched from remote sites, and must be delivered. Error

(apiV1StatusesIdRebloggedByGet)

post /api/v1/statuses
(apiV1StatusesPost)

Consumes

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/json

Request body

_api_v1_statuses_post_request_inner _api_v1_statuses_post_request_inner (optional)
Body Parameter —

Request headers

Idempotency-Key (optional)
Header Parameter — Prevent duplicate submissions of the same status. Idempotency keys are stored for up to 1 hour, and can be any arbitrary string. Consider using a hash or UUID generated client-side. default: null

Return type

_api_v1_statuses_post_200_response

get /api/v1/timelines/list/{list_id}
(apiV1TimelinesListListIdGet)
View statuses in the given list timeline.

Path parameters

list_id (required)
Path Parameter — Local ID of the list in the database. default: null

Query parameters

limit (optional)
Query Parameter — Max number of results to return. Defaults to 20. default: 20
max_id (optional)
Query Parameter — Return results older than ID default: null
since_id (optional)
Query Parameter — Return results newer than ID default: null
min_id (optional)
Query Parameter — Return results immediately newer than ID default: null

401

(apiV1TimelinesPublicGet)

Query parameters

local (optional)
Query Parameter — Show only local statuses? Defaults to false. default: false
remote (optional)
Query Parameter — Show only local statuses? Defaults to false. default: false
only_media (optional)

since_id (optional)
Query Parameter — Return results newer than ID default: null

Query Parameter — Return results immediately newer than ID default: null

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

get statuses.
Up 
get /api/v1/timelines/tag/{hashtag}
(apiV1TimelinesTagHashtagGet)
View public statuses containing the given hashtag.

Path parameters

hashtag (required)
Path Parameter — Content of a #hashtag``, not including #` symbol.. default: null

Query parameters

local (optional)
Query Parameter — Show only local statuses? Defaults to false. default: false
remote (optional)
Query Parameter — Show only local statuses? Defaults to false. default: false
only_media (optional)
Query Parameter — Show only statuses with media attached? Defaults to false.. default: false
limit (optional)
Query Parameter — Max number of results to return. Defaults to 20. default: 20
max_id (optional)
Query Parameter — Return results older than ID default: null
since_id (optional)
Query Parameter — Return results newer than ID default: null
min_id (optional)
Query Parameter — Return results immediately newer than ID default: null

Return type

array[Status]

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

Get statuses.
Up 
get /api/v1/trends
(apiV1TrendsGet)
Tags that are being used more frequently within the past week.

Query parameters

limit (optional)
Query Parameter — Max number of results to return. Defaults to 10. default: 10

Return type

array[Tag]

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
[ {
  "name" : "name",
  "history" : [ {
    "uses" : "uses",
    "accounts" : "accounts",
    "day" : "day"
  }, {

    "accounts" : "accounts",
    "day" : "day"
  } ],
  "url" : "url"
}, {
  "name" : "name",
  "history" : [ {
    "uses" : "uses",
    "accounts" : "accounts",
    "day" : "day"
  }, {
    "uses" : "uses",
    "accounts" : "accounts",
    "day" : "day"
  } ],
  "url" : "url"
} ]

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

Domains that this instance is aware of.
Up 
get /api/v2/search
(apiV2SearchGet)
Search results

Query parameters

q (required)
Query Parameter — What to search for default: null
limit (optional)
Query Parameter — Maximum number of results. Defaults to 40. default: 20
resolve (optional)
Query Parameter — Attempt WebFinger lookup. default: null
following (optional)
Query Parameter — Only who the user is following. Defaults to false. default: null
account_id (optional)
Query Parameter — If provided, statuses returned will be authored only by this account default: null
max_id (optional)
Query Parameter — Return results older than this id default: null
min_id (optional)
Query Parameter — Return results immediately newer than this id default: null
type (optional)
Query Parameter — Enum(accounts, hashtags, statuses) default: null
exclude_unreviewed (optional)
Query Parameter — Filter out unreviewed tags? Defaults to false. Use true when trying to find trending tags. default: null
offset (optional)
Query Parameter — Offset in search results. Used for pagination. Defaults to 0. default: null

Return type

_api_v2_search_get_200_response

Oauth

Up 
get /oauth/authorize
(oauthAuthorizeGet)
Displays an authorization form to the user. If approved, it will create and return an authorization code, then redirect to the desired redirect_uri, or show the authorization code if urn:ietf:wg:oauth:2.0:oob was requested. The authorization code can be used while requesting a token to obtain access to user-level methods.

Query parameters

response_type (required)
Query Parameter — Should be set equal to code. default: null
client_id (required)
Query Parameter — Client ID, obtained during app registration. default: null
redirect_uri (required)
Query Parameter — Set a URI to redirect the user to. If this parameter is set to urn:ietf:wg:oauth:2.0:oob then the authorization code will be shown instead. Must match one of the redirect URIs declared during app registration. default: null
scope (optional)
Query Parameter — List of requested OAuth scopes, separated by spaces (or by pluses, if using query parameters). Must be a subset of scopes declared during app registration. If not provided, defaults to read. default: null
force_login (optional)
Query Parameter — Added in 2.6.0. Forces the user to re-login, which is necessary for authorizing with multiple accounts from the same instance. default: null

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "error_description" : "error_description",
  "error" : "error"
}

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

The authorization code will be returned as a query parameter named code.

400

If the authorization code is incorrect or has been used already, the request will fail. Error
Up 
post /oauth/revoke
(oauthRevokePost)
Revoke an access token to make it no longer valid for use.

Consumes

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/form-data

Request body

_oauth_revoke_post_request _oauth_revoke_post_request (optional)
Body Parameter —

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "error_description" : "error_description",
  "error" : "error"
}

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

If you own the provided token, the API call will provide an empty response. This operation is idempotent, so calling this API multiple times will still return OK.

403

If you provide a token you do not own, or no token at all, the API call will return a 403 error. Error
Up 
post /oauth/token
(oauthTokenPost)
Returns an access token, to be used during API calls that are not public.

Consumes

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/form-data

Request body

_oauth_token_post_request _oauth_token_post_request (optional)
Body Parameter —

Return type

_oauth_token_post_200_response

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "access_token" : "ZA-Yj3aBD8U8Cm7lKUp-lm9O9BmDgdhHzDeqsY8tlL0",
  "scope" : "read write follow push",
  "created_at" : 1573979017,
  "token_type" : "Bearer"
}

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "error_description" : "error_description",
  "error" : "error"
}

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "error_description" : "error_description",
  "error" : "error"
}

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

Store this access_token for later use with auth-required methods. The token should be passed as an HTTP Authorization header when making API calls, with the value Bearer access_token _oauth_token_post_200_response

400

If you try to request a scope that was not included when registering the app, the request will fail. Error

401

If client_id and client_secret do not match or are invalid, the request will fail. Error

TODOSecurity

Up 
post /api/v1/accounts
(apiV1AccountsPost)
Creates a user and account records. Returns an account access token for the app that initiated the request. The app should save this token for later, and should wait for the user to confirm their account by clicking a link in their email inbox.

Consumes

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/form-data

Request body

_api_v1_accounts_post_request _api_v1_accounts_post_request (optional)
Body Parameter —

Responses

200

Success

401

Unauthorized

Account - Up

Represents a user of Mastodon and their associated profile.
acct (optional)
String The Webfinger account URI. Equal to username for local users, or username@domain for
avatar (optional)
String An image icon that is shown next to statuses and in the profile. The format is URL.
avatar_static (optional)
String A static version of the avatar. Equal to avatar if its value is a static image; different if avatar is an animated GIF. The format is URL.
bot (optional)
Boolean A presentational flag. Indicates that the account may perform automated actions, may not be monitored, or identifies as a robot.
created_at (optional)
Date When the account was created. format: date-time
discoverable (optional)
Boolean Whether the account has opted into discovery features such as the profile directory.
display_name (optional)
String The profile's display name.
emojis (optional)
array[Emoji] Custom emoji entities to be used when rendering the profile. If none, an empty array will be returned.
fields (optional)
array[Field] Additional metadata attached to a profile as name-value pairs.
followers_count (optional)
Integer The reported followers of this profile.
following_count (optional)
Integer The reported follows of this profile.
header (optional)
String An image banner that is shown above the profile and in profile cards. The format is URL.
header_static (optional)
String A static version of the header. Equal to header if its value is a static image; different if header is an animated GIF. The format is URL.
id (optional)
String The account id header.
last_status_at (optional)
Date When the most recent status was posted. format: date-time
locked (optional)
Boolean Whether the account manually approves follow requests.
moved (optional)
Account
mute_expires_at (optional)
Date When a timed mute will expire, if applicable. ISO 8601 Datetime. format: date-time
note (optional)
String The profile's bio / description.
source (optional)
Source
statuses_count (optional)
Integer How many statuses are attached to this account.
suspended (optional)
Boolean An extra entity returned when an account is suspended.
url (optional)
String The location of the user's profile page. (HTTPS URL)
username (optional)
String The username of the account, not including domain.

Activity - Up

Represents a weekly bucket of instance activity.
logins (optional)
String User logins since the week began, String (cast from an integer).
registrations (optional)
String User registrations since the week began, String (cast from an integer).
statuses (optional)
String Statuses created since the week began, String (cast from an integer).
week (optional)
String Midnight at the first day of the week. (UNIX Timestamp).

array[oas_any_type_not_mapped] Possible answers for the poll.
own_votes (optional)
array[Integer] When called with a user token, which options has the authorized user chosen? Contains an array of index values for options. Array of Number, or null if no current user
voted (optional)
Boolean When called with a user token, has the authorized user voted? Boolean, or null if no current user
voters_count (optional)
Integer How many unique accounts have voted on a multiple-choice poll. Number, or null if multiple is false.
votes_count (optional)
Integer How many votes have been received.

_api_v1_statuses_post_request_inner - Up

in_reply_to_id (optional)
String ID of the status being replied to, if status is a reply
language (optional)
String ISO 639 language code for this status.
media_ids (optional)
array[String] Array of Attachment ids to be attached as media. If provided, status becomes optional, and poll cannot be used.
poll (optional)
map[Object]
scheduled_at (optional)
String ISO 8601 Datetime at which to schedule a status. Providing this paramter will cause ScheduledStatus to be returned instead of Status. Must be at least 5 minutes in the future.
sensitive (optional)
Boolean Mark status and attached media as sensitive?
spoiler_text (optional)
String Text to be shown as a warning or subject before the actual content. Statuses are generally collapsed behind this field.
status (optional)
String Text content of the status. If media_ids is provided, this becomes optional. Attaching a poll is optional while status is provided.
visibility (optional)
String Visibility of the posted status. Enumerable oneOf public, unlisted, private, direct.
Enum:
public
unlisted
private
direct

_oauth_token_post_request - Up

client_id
String Client ID, obtained during app registration
client_secret
String Client secret, obtained during app registration
code (optional)
String A user authorization code, obtained via /oauth/authorize
grant_type
String Set equal to authorization_code if code is provided in order to gain user-level access. Otherwise, set equal to client_credentials to obtain app-level access only.
redirect_uri
String Set a URI to redirect the user to. If this parameter is set to urn:ietf:wg:oauth:2.0:oob then the token will be shown instead. Must match one of the redirect URIs declared during app registration.
scopes (optional)
String List of requested OAuth scopes, separated by spaces. Must be a subset of scopes declared during app registration. If not provided, defaults to read.
